# pi-loom

A [Pi Coding Agent](https://pi.dev) extension that introduces **loom**, a
purpose-built scripting language for authoring parameterized, programmatic
templates that drive an LLM conversation.

A `.loom` file interleaves ordinary code (variables, loops, conditionals,
functions) with literal text destined for the model. Evaluating a loom
appends turns to a conversation — either the caller's current conversation
(*prompt mode*) or a fresh isolated conversation (*subagent mode*) — and
evaluates to a final value (its last expression or `return expr`),
available to programmatic callers and propagated across the subagent
boundary. Loom evaluation itself produces no file outputs; any file writes
occur only through Pi tools the loom explicitly admits via frontmatter
`tools:` (e.g. `write`, `edit`). `.warp` files are library modules that
share loom's grammar and type system and are imported by `.loom` files.

The full design lives in [`docs/spec.md`](./docs/spec.md). The implementation roadmap
lives in [`docs/plan.md`](./docs/plan.md).

## Status

Implementation in progress. Track progress against
[`docs/plan.md`](./docs/plan.md) and the
[spec coverage matrix](./docs/plan_topics/coverage-matrix.md).

| Leaf | Status | Date | Notes |
| H8a-T | Tests red | 2026-07-02 | Live production end-to-end acceptance tests (paired `H8a` impl; Convention. — live-host acceptance pair exception; extension-bootstrap-and-per-loom.md, registration-steps.md, discovery.md). Adds an OPT-IN live-host acceptance suite excluded from the default `npm test` and invoked by the dedicated `npm run test:live` runner (`vitest.live.config.ts`; default `vitest.config.ts` excludes `tests/live/**`). `tests/live/harness.ts` boots a REAL `AgentSession` (via the SDK `createAgentSession` + `DefaultResourceLoader` with `noExtensions` + `additionalExtensionPaths: [extensions/index.ts]`) loading loom through its SHIPPED entry (re-exporting the `src/**` factory), plants real `.loom` files under the project source `<cwd>/.pi/looms/` and a `--loom <dir>` CLI source, fires `session_start`, and can drive live turns; `requireLiveProvider()` fails loudly naming the missing precondition when no provider/model is configured (never a silent skip), preferring a fast/cheap model. `tests/live/live-production-acceptance.test.ts` — four Convention (live-host acceptance) bullets: (1) discovery→registration (project source), (2) prompt-mode turn against a live model asserting the deterministic sentinel, (3) alternate discovery source (`--loom` CLI), (4) bounded typed-query lowering validated against its declared schema via the production `AjvSchemaValidator` (V5d). Each test asserts the discovered command exists BEFORE any live turn, so the intended-reason red spends no tokens. No `src/**` change; no new diagnostics-registry codes. Typecheck clean; default suite 1391 green; run under `npm run test:live` with a configured provider, all 4 tests red on their own primary assertion (`expect(command).toBeDefined()` → `Registered: []`) because the shipped production composition root supplies `fixtures: []` and runs no discovery walk — fail-red-for-the-intended-reason, not a credential/network/setup/harness throw. Paired `H8a` wires the production composition root and turns these green. |
| V9r | Complete | 2026-07-02 | Session-swap fail-fast tripwire (paired with `V9r-T`; pi-integration-contract/session-only-degraded-state.md §Session-swap fail-fast tripwire, host-prerequisites.md clause (a) `governed-by-rebind` / (b) / (c-i) / (d), diagnostics/code-registry-host.md). Fills the four behaviour-bearing seams in `src/extension/session-swap-tripwire.ts` and wires the arming into `src/extension/session-shutdown.ts`. `sessionSwapInstanceSurvivedDiagnostic(reason)` builds the (E, runtime) diagnostic with `details.event.reason` = the armed session-only reason and the *Message* string sourced verbatim from diagnostics/code-registry-host.md (`<reason>` interpolated, em-dash separator). `armSessionSwapTripwireForReason(registry, reason)` arms the private per-instance `sessionSwapTornDown` flag only when `isSessionOnlyReason` (`"new"`/`"resume"`/`"fork"`), a no-op on `"quit"`/`"reload"` or an unknown coerced reason, idempotent under multi-`session_shutdown` delivery (clause (b)). `guardSessionSwapTripwire(deps)` fires only on the ARMED tripwire — emit exactly one `loom/host/session-swap-instance-survived` via the `console.error` sink, then fail-fast-terminate (control does not return); a no-op when unarmed (dormant governed-by-rebind steady state). `runGuardedSlashHandler(deps, dispatch)` runs the guard at entry so an armed tripwire terminates before `dispatch` ever runs; the Pi-owned `/reload` is never wrapped and stays unguarded (clause (c-i)). `runSessionShutdown` calls `armSessionSwapTripwireForReason` after the full five-sub-step teardown, writing NO degraded branch (no `markRuntimeDegraded`, no `"degraded-needs-reload"` tag, no `session-shutdown-runtime-degraded` emission, no degraded slash note). No new diagnostics-registry codes; the guard emission reuses `V9g`'s `emitTeardownDiagnostic` (its existing allow-broad-catch sites). No module-level mutable state / broad catch / ambient primitive / Promise combinator / `Sync` call in `src/**`. All 13 `V9r-T` tests green; full suite 1385 green, typecheck + lint + H2a/H3a gates clean. |

No new diagnostics-registry codes (the host row already exists; `V9r-T` is its first asserting test). Inert/non-compliant stub seam: no module-level mutable state / broad catch / ambient primitive / Promise combinator / `Sync` call; the guard's emission reuses `V9g`'s `emitTeardownDiagnostic` (its existing allow-broad-catch sites). Typecheck + lint clean; 10 of the 13 tests red on their own primary assertions (sentinel diagnostic, absent arming, inverted/absent guard, unguarded dispatch) because the `V9r` body is absent — fail-red-for-the-intended-reason; the 3 companion tests (negative arming for quit/reload, the `isSessionOnlyReason` predicate, dormant guarded dispatch) hold as steady-state invariants; the other 1375 tests stay green. |
| V9g | Complete | 2026-07-01 | Session-shutdown teardown + emission isolation (paired with `V9g-T`; pi-integration-contract/session-shutdown-semantics.md, diagnostic-emission-isolation.md, cancellation.md). Fills the behaviour-bearing seams in `src/extension/session-shutdown.ts`. `runSessionShutdown(event, deps)` runs the five-sub-step fixed teardown with per-step isolation: sub-step 1 `drain()`→`initDrainStateTag()` (fixed order, each in its own `try`/`catch`); sub-step 2 stamps each in-flight entry's `shutdownReason` then aborts its `loomAbort` with the synthesised CNCL-4 `Error` (byte-exact `"loom cancelled by session shutdown"`, observable as `signal.reason === source.reason`), per-entry isolation, no diagnostic; sub-step 3 the cka-31 bounded settle-all — `Promise.allSettled` over every entry's `disposeBarrier` raced against a `Clock.setTimeout(SHUTDOWN_AWAIT_CAP_MS)` cap (deadline-capture `Clock.now()` + cap-arming `setTimeout` each isolated; a cap-arm throw degrades to a skipped await, not an unbounded one), emitting one `reload-teardown-timeout` naming the still-in-flight entries in insertion order at the cap and clearing the timer on the clean path; sub-step 4 closes both watchers + clears the debounce handle (three isolated call sites); sub-step 5 detaches every forwarding listener (isolated). Still-in-flight tracking uses a synchronous per-barrier `.then` drop-set so the cap timer decides accurately regardless of `Promise.allSettled`'s internal microtask hops. `emitTeardownDiagnostic` wraps the flat-`details` serialise-then-`console.error` sequence (PIC-24) with a bare-`code` fallback on serialiser throw (PIC-25) and swallows an emit throw with no retry (PIC-27, `serialiseOk`-gated); `emitNestedShapeDiagnostic` adds the two-token `${code} ${reason}` serialiser-throw fallback and the construction-site self-wrap emitting the two-token `${code} <unreadable>` / three-token `${code} ${entry.loom} <unreadable>` forms with a dedicated inner swallow (PIC-26). Builders `teardownStepFailedDiagnostic` (`{step,call,error}`, `<unreadable>`-fallback underlying-error coercion), `reloadTeardownTimeoutDiagnostic` (elapsed `<ms>` + bare-integer `hint`, `/<name>:<uuid>` `, `-joined list), `cancelledBySessionShutdownDiagnostic` (nested `details.event.{reason,loom,invocation_id}`). Reason capture is `String`-coerced with an `"<unreadable>"` fallback; the full four-arm Unknown-reason routing stays owned by `V9h`. The eleven spec-mandated broad-`catch` sites (per-step isolation + diagnostic-emission isolation, conventions sites 4/5) carry `// allow-broad-catch: PIC-7`; `Promise.allSettled` carries `// allow: cka-31`. No new diagnostics-registry codes. No module-level mutable state / ambient primitive / `Sync` call. All 27 `V9g-T` tests green; typecheck + lint (incl. `no-broad-catch` / `no-restricted-syntax`) clean; full suite green apart from the 4 pre-existing `V4g-T` reds in an unrelated subsystem (`tests/pre-evaluation-reload-failure.test.ts`, red on HEAD without this change). |

Panics bypass `?` (`evaluateQuestion` invokes the operand outside any catch, so a thrown panic propagates) and `match` (a panic is a thrown value, never an arm selection). `evaluateQuestion` applies `?` propagation: `Ok(v)`→`value`, `Err(e)`→`propagate`. `surfaceUnexpectedThrow` routes an unexpected throw to `loom/runtime/internal-error` (`internal error: <error.message>`, `hint`=`error.stack` or `"<no stack available>"`), passes a `LoomPanic` through unreclassified (`undefined`), and emits no diagnostic for a NOCEIL-3 `HostFatal`. | V3a | Complete | 2026-06-30 | Expression evaluator (paired with `V3a-T`): fills `src/runtime/expression-evaluator.ts`. A self-contained tokenizer + recursive-descent parser + tree-walking evaluator for the bounded TypeScript subset of expressions.md §"Supported forms" exercised by V3a (number/string/boolean/null literals, identifier reads, `name(args)` calls, unary `!`/`-`, binary `+ - * / %` / `< <= > >=` / `== !=`, logical `&&`/`||`, ternary `?:`, parens). Precedence/associativity follow the §"Operator precedence" table (highest→lowest: primary/call, unary right-assoc, `* / %` left, `+ -` left, ordering non-assoc, equality non-assoc, `&&` left, `||` left, ternary right-assoc). Evaluation is left-to-right with `&&`/`||` short-circuit and ternary branch-selection routed through `EvalHost.callFunction`, so a short-circuited / not-taken operand's call never runs (§"Evaluation order and short-circuiting"). `==`/`!=` route through the V2c `valuesEqual` structural relation (cross-type → `false`/`true`, no panic; `42 == 42.0` → `true`); `+` concatenates two strings else adds; `-`/`*`/`%` numeric; `/` always `number`; div/mod-by-zero use the host's native IEEE-754 (`1/0`→`Infinity`, `0/0`/`5%0`→`NaN`) with no panic; ordering uses the host relational operators (signed numeric / UTF-16 code-unit, `NaN`→`false`). `checkBooleanPosition` routes the operand type through the V2b `⊑` relation against `boolean` and fires `loom/parse/non-boolean-condition` ("condition must be boolean; got <type>", message anchored to code-registry-parse.md) for any non-`boolean`, deferring a statically-unresolvable operand to the runtime safety net. No module-level mutable state (the operator constants are immutable), no broad catch / ambient primitive / Promise combinator / Sync call. All 21 `V3a-T` tests green; full suite 345 green, typecheck + lint clean; H2a/H3a scans green. |

| V2d | Complete | 2026-06-30 | Canonical integer/number renderer (paired with `V2d-T`): fills `src/render/canonical-number.ts`. `renderCanonicalNumber(value, kind)` selects BNDR-4 (`integer`) vs BNDR-5 (`number`) from the caller-supplied `kind` discriminator — never the value's runtime integrality — and depends on no value model or schema. A shared `expandToFixedPoint` re-expands `String(n)`'s exponential form (the forbidden `±1e21` large-magnitude and `\|value\| < 1e-7` small-magnitude switches) to pure fixed-point by shifting the decimal point, leaving non-exponential shortest digits untouched; `canonicalDecimal` adds sign handling and the `-0 → 0` pin (`value === 0` covers `+0`/`-0`). BNDR-4: `42`→`42`, `0`→`0`, `-7`→`-7`, `1e21`→`1000000000000000000000` (no exponent/separators), `-0`→`0` (bndr-6p). BNDR-5: `3.14`→`3.14` (bndr-6q), integral `42`→`42` (no `.0`), `1e21`→`1000000000000000000000` (bndr-6r), `1e-8`→`0.00000001` (bndr-6s), interior `5e-8`→`0.00000005`, `-0`→`0` (bndr-6p). Cat 1 `renderType` re-serialises a Loom static type in source-grammar form (lowercase primitives, `\| `-joined unions, `array<T>`, `Result<T, E>`, inline object `{ f: T }`). Cat 2 `renderRuntimeValue` stringifies via the canonical table with the 80→77+`...` code-point truncation (counted by code point) and `Ok(…)`/`Err(…)`. Cat 3 `renderConstruct` emits the caller-supplied closed token-name / verbatim span. Cat 4 `renderInteger` is shortest-decimal with `-0`→`0`. Cat 5 `renderSourceDerived` renders identifiers/paths bare, `<key>` quoted only when not identifier-shaped (`^[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*$`), `<char>` raw-or-escaped (`\xNN`/`\u{NNNN}`), `<descriptor>` as `<kind>:"<value>"`. Cat 6 `renderUnderlyingError` coerces a caught throw (object string `.message`, else `String(v)`, else `<unreadable>`) then first-line-truncates (`\r\n`/`\r`→`\n`, cut at first `\n`, trailing-ws preserved, `<no message>` when empty; `\u2028`/`\u2029` ordinary). Cat 7 `renderCategory7` dispatches the closed sub-rules (identifier/closed-enum verbatim, `<uuid>` lowercased, numeric via cat 4, path/descriptor via cat 5). Cat 8 `renderHostDerivedTail`/`renderHostIncompatible` assemble the `host incompatible (<kind>): observed <observed>, required <required>` template with the host-derived `<observed>` first-line-truncated; host version passed in, never read from `process`. All 10 `V7c-T` tests green; full suite 133 green, typecheck + lint clean. |
| V7c-T | Tests red | 2026-06-30 | Placeholder-rendering tests (paired `V7c` impl): the `src/diagnostics/placeholder.ts` seam (eight per-category render functions — `renderType`, `renderRuntimeValue`, `renderConstruct`, `renderInteger`, `renderSourceDerived`, `renderUnderlyingError`, `renderCategory7`, `renderHostDerivedTail` / `renderHostIncompatible` — inert stubs returning `""`) plus `tests/placeholder-rendering.test.ts` with ten failing tests pinning `DIAG-4`: each of the eight categories renders its normative vector byte-identically (static-type re-serialisation; runtime-value stringification; construct closed-token + verbatim span; integer rule; source-derived verbatim; underlying-error first-line coercion; category-7 closed-enum/uuid/numeric; category-8 host-derived tail), the category-2 80→81 code-point truncation boundary (full at 80, `77 chars + "..."` at 81), and the category-8 `loom/load/host-incompatible` (`node-floor`) row with the host version mocked to `v18.19.0` asserted via the §8 anchored partial-match `^host incompatible \(node-floor\): observed (.*), required >=22\.19\.0$` (the *Message* template sourced from the registry, never a full-*Message* equality). (per-finding fixes processed bottom-up by `/fix-spec-shape-single-findings`).

## Highlights

- **Two file kinds, one grammar.** `.loom` files are invocable as Pi slash
  commands; `.warp` files are import-only library modules.
- **Query-and-await.** `@`-prefixed templates send the conversation so far to
  the model and bind the typed reply to a variable.
- **Structured outputs.** `schema` declarations lower to a JSON-Schema subset
  validated with AJV; typed queries return `Result<T, QueryError>`.
- **Two execution modes.** *Prompt mode* appends to the caller's
  conversation; *subagent mode* runs in an isolated child conversation and
  returns a value.
- **Tool calls and cross-loom invocation.** `<tool>(args)` invokes registered
  Pi tools; `invoke(...)` runs another loom with cycle detection.
- **LLM-driven argument binding.** Slash-command arguments are parsed into
  typed `params` by an LLM binder with deterministic fallbacks.

## Install

Not yet published. Once implemented, the extension will be installed as a Pi
package that exposes its `extensions/` directory via the `pi.extensions`
field in `package.json`.

## Repository layout

| Path | Contents |
|---|---|
| [`docs/spec.md`](./docs/spec.md) | Top-level spec index. |
| [`docs/spec_topics/`](./docs/spec_topics/) | Per-topic normative spec pages. |
| [`docs/plan.md`](./docs/plan.md) | Top-level implementation plan. |
| [`docs/plan_topics/`](./docs/plan_topics/) | Per-phase plan pages and coverage matrix. |
| [`docs/spec-review.md`](./docs/spec-review.md) | Spec review log. |
| `extensions/` | Pi extension entry points (populated during implementation). |
| `package.json` | Package manifest; declares the Pi extension and peer-deps on `@earendil-works/pi-*`. |
